They represent the overall\n  // signature of the board.\n  const outputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n\n  // Analyze inputs and remember some things about them that we'll need when we\n  // traverse the outputs.\n  const inputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n  const inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo = new Map<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort,\n    { nodeId: string; portName: string }\n  >();\n\n  const unconnectedInputs = new Set<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort\n  >();\n\n  const inputsArray = (\n    Array.isArray(board.inputsForSerialization)\n      ? input.id : undefined) ??\n        autoId();\n\n      inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo.set(input, {\n        nodeId: inputNodeId,\n        portName: mainInputName,\n      });\n      unconnectedInputs.add(input);\n      const { schema, required } = describeInput(input);\n      let inputNode = inputNodes.get(inputNodeId);\n      if (inputNode === undefined) {\n        inputNode = {\n          id: inputNodeId,\n          type: \"input\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const metadata = inputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (metadata !== undefined) {\n          inputNode.metadata = metadata;\n        }\n        inputNodes.set(inputNodeId, inputNode);\n      }\n      const normalizedSchema = sortKeys(schema, [\n        \"type\",\n        \"behavior\",\n        \"title\",\n        \"description\",\n        \"default\",\n        \"examples\",\n        \"anyOf\",\n        \"properties\",\n        \"items\",\n        \"required\",\n        \"additionalProperties\",\n      ]);\n      if (mainInputName === \"*\") {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.additionalProperties = normalizedSchema;\n      } else {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.properties[mainInputName] =\n          normalizedSchema;\n        if (required) {\n          inputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(mainInputName);\n        }\n      }\n      if (isSpecialInput(input)) {\n        magicInputResolutions.set(input, {\n          nodeId: inputNodeId,\n          portName: mainInputName,\n        });\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const outputsArray = Array.isArray(board.outputsForSerialization)\n    ? (isBoardOutput(port) ? port : undefined);\n\n      if (isSerializableOutputPortReference(port)) {\n        port = port[OutputPortGetter];\n      }\n      // TODO(aomarks) Remove cast.\n      outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n        outputNode = {\n          id: outputNodeId,\n          type: \"output\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const nodeMetadata = outputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (nodeMetadata !== undefined) {\n          outputNode.metadata = nodeMetadata;\n        }\n        if (outputs.$bubble) {\n          addBehavior(outputNode.configuration.schema, \"bubble\");\n        }\n\n        outputNodes.set(outputNodeId, outputNode);\n      }\n      const { schema, required } = describeOutput(output);\n      outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n        `Board input \"${inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo.get(input)!.portName}\" ` +\n          `is not reachable from any of its outputs.`\n      );\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (board.describer) {\n    const describerId = embedBoardAndReturnItsId(board.describer);\n    board.metadata ??= {};\n    board.metadata.describer = `#${describerId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (errors.length > 0) {\n    // TODO(aomarks) Refactor this to a version: board.version } : {}),\n    ...(board.metadata ? { metadata: board.metadata } : {}),\n    // Sort the nodes and edges for deterministic BGL output.\n    edges: edges.sort((a, b) => {\n      if (a.from != b.from) {\n        return a.from.localeCompare(b.from);\n      }\n      if (a.to != b.to) {\n        return a.to.localeCompare(b.to);\n      }\n      if (a.out != b.out) {\n SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n An inport port\n          // value can never actually be undefined, right?\n          throw new Error(\n            `Internal error: value was undefined for a ${inputPort.node?.type}:${inputPort.name} port.`\n          );\n        } else if (typeof value === \"symbol\") {\n          // TODO(aomarks) Why is this possible in the type system? Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}

They represent the overall\n  // signature of the board.\n  const outputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n\n  // Analyze inputs and remember some things about them that we'll need when we\n  // traverse the outputs.\n  const inputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n  const inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo = new Map<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort,\n    { nodeId: string; portName: string }\n  >();\n\n  const unconnectedInputs = new Set<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort\n  >();\n\n  const inputsArray = (\n    Array.isArray(board.inputsForSerialization)\n      ? input.id : undefined) ??\n        autoId();\n\n      inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo.set(input, {\n        nodeId: inputNodeId,\n        portName: mainInputName,\n      });\n      unconnectedInputs.add(input);\n      const { schema, required } = describeInput(input);\n      let inputNode = inputNodes.get(inputNodeId);\n      if (inputNode === undefined) {\n        inputNode = {\n          id: inputNodeId,\n          type: \"input\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const metadata = inputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (metadata !== undefined) {\n          inputNode.metadata = metadata;\n        }\n        inputNodes.set(inputNodeId, inputNode);\n      }\n      const normalizedSchema = sortKeys(schema, [\n        \"type\",\n        \"behavior\",\n        \"title\",\n        \"description\",\n        \"default\",\n        \"examples\",\n        \"anyOf\",\n        \"properties\",\n        \"items\",\n        \"required\",\n        \"additionalProperties\",\n      ]);\n      if (mainInputName === \"*\") {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.additionalProperties = normalizedSchema;\n      } else {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.properties[mainInputName] =\n          normalizedSchema;\n        if (required) {\n          inputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(mainInputName);\n        }\n      }\n      if (isSpecialInput(input)) {\n        magicInputResolutions.set(input, {\n          nodeId: inputNodeId,\n          portName: mainInputName,\n        });\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const outputsArray = Array.isArray(board.outputsForSerialization)\n    ? (isBoardOutput(port) ? port : undefined);\n\n      if (isSerializableOutputPortReference(port)) {\n        port = port[OutputPortGetter];\n      }\n      // TODO(aomarks) Remove cast.\n      outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n        outputNode = {\n          id: outputNodeId,\n          type: \"output\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const nodeMetadata = outputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (nodeMetadata !== undefined) {\n          outputNode.metadata = nodeMetadata;\n        }\n        if (outputs.$bubble) {\n          addBehavior(outputNode.configuration.schema, \"bubble\");\n        }\n\n        outputNodes.set(outputNodeId, outputNode);\n      }\n      const { schema, required } = describeOutput(output);\n      outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n        `Board input \"${inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo.get(input)!.portName}\" ` +\n          `is not reachable from any of its outputs.`\n      );\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (board.describer) {\n    const describerId = embedBoardAndReturnItsId(board.describer);\n    board.metadata ??= {};\n    board.metadata.describer = `#${describerId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (errors.length > 0) {\n    // TODO(aomarks) Refactor this to a Result<> return, because these errors are\n    // expected as part of the normal course of operation.\n    throw new Error(\n      `Error serializing board:\\n\\n${errors.sort().join(\"\\n\\n\")}`\n version: board.version } : {}),\n    ...(board.metadata ? { metadata: board.metadata } : {}),\n    // Sort the nodes and edges for deterministic BGL output.\n    edges: edges.sort((a, b) => {\n      if (a.from != b.from) {\n        return a.from.localeCompare(b.from);\n      }\n      if (a.to != b.to) {\n        return a.to.localeCompare(b.to);\n      }\n      if (a.out != b.out) {\n SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n important we add the node to the nodes map before we next\n    // recurse, or else we can get stuck in a loop.\n    nodes.set(node, descriptor);\n\n    const configurationEntries: Array<[string, An inport port\n          // value can never actually be undefined, right?\n          throw new Error(\n            `Internal error: value was undefined for a ${inputPort.node?.type}:${inputPort.name} port.`\n          );\n        } else if (typeof value === \"symbol\") {\n          // TODO(aomarks) Why is this possible in the type system? Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}

outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n        outputNode = {\n          id: outputNodeId,\n          type: \"output\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}

They represent the overall\n  // signature of the board.\n  const outputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n\n  // Analyze inputs and remember some things about them that we'll need when we\n  // traverse the outputs.\n  const inputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n  const inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo = new Map<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort,\n    { nodeId: string; portName: string }\n  >();\n\n  const unconnectedInputs = new Set<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort\n  >();\n\n  const inputsArray = (\n    Array.isArray(board.inputsForSerialization)\n      ? input.id : undefined) ??\n        autoId();\n\n      inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo.set(input, {\n        nodeId: inputNodeId,\n        portName: mainInputName,\n      });\n      unconnectedInputs.add(input);\n      const { schema, required } = describeInput(input);\n      let inputNode = inputNodes.get(inputNodeId);\n      if (inputNode === undefined) {\n        inputNode = {\n          id: inputNodeId,\n          type: \"input\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const metadata = inputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (metadata !== undefined) {\n          inputNode.metadata = metadata;\n        }\n        inputNodes.set(inputNodeId, inputNode);\n      }\n      const normalizedSchema = sortKeys(schema, [\n        \"type\",\n        \"behavior\",\n        \"title\",\n        \"description\",\n        \"default\",\n        \"examples\",\n        \"anyOf\",\n        \"properties\",\n        \"items\",\n        \"required\",\n        \"additionalProperties\",\n      ]);\n      if (mainInputName === \"*\") {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.additionalProperties = normalizedSchema;\n      } else {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.properties[mainInputName] =\n          normalizedSchema;\n        if (required) {\n          inputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(mainInputName);\n        }\n      }\n      if (isSpecialInput(input)) {\n        magicInputResolutions.set(input, {\n          nodeId: inputNodeId,\n          portName: mainInputName,\n        });\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const outputsArray = Array.isArray(board.outputsForSerialization)\n    ? (isBoardOutput(port) ? port : undefined);\n\n      if (isSerializableOutputPortReference(port)) {\n        port = port[OutputPortGetter];\n      }\n      // TODO(aomarks) Remove cast.\n      outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n        outputNode = {\n          id: outputNodeId,\n          type: \"output\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const nodeMetadata = outputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (nodeMetadata !== undefined) {\n          outputNode.metadata = nodeMetadata;\n        }\n        if (outputs.$bubble) {\n          addBehavior(outputNode.configuration.schema, \"bubble\");\n        }\n\n        outputNodes.set(outputNodeId, outputNode);\n      }\n      const { schema, required } = describeOutput(output);\n      outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if (isSpecialInput(port)) {\n        unconnectedInputs.delete(port);\n        const resolution = magicInputResolutions.get(port);\n        if (resolution !== undefined) {\n          addEdge(\n            resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n        `Board input \"${inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo.get(input)!.portName}\" ` +\n          `is not reachable from any of its outputs.`\n      );\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (board.describer) {\n    const describerId = embedBoardAndReturnItsId(board.describer);\n    board.metadata ??= {};\n    board.metadata.describer = `#${describerId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (errors.length > 0) {\n    // TODO(aomarks) Refactor this to a Result<> return, because these errors are\n    // expected as part of the normal course of operation.\n    throw new Error(\n      `Error serializing board:\\n\\n${errors.sort().join(\"\\n\\n\")}`\n version: board.version } : {}),\n    ...(board.metadata ? { metadata: board.metadata } : {}),\n    // Sort the nodes and edges for deterministic BGL output.\n    edges: edges.sort((a, b) => {\n      if (a.from != b.from) {\n        return a.from.localeCompare(b.from);\n      }\n      if (a.to != b.to) {\n        return a.to.localeCompare(b.to);\n      }\n      if (a.out != b.out) {\n SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n An inport port\n          // value can never actually be undefined, right?\n          throw new Error(\n            `Internal error: value was undefined for a ${inputPort.node?.type}:${inputPort.name} port.`\n          );\n        } else if (typeof value === \"symbol\") {\n          // TODO(aomarks) Why is this possible in the type system? Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}

They represent the overall\n  // signature of the board.\n  const outputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n\n  // Analyze inputs and remember some things about them that we'll need when we\n  // traverse the outputs.\n  const inputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n  const inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo = new Map<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort,\n    { nodeId: string; portName: string }\n  >();\n\n  const unconnectedInputs = new Set<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort\n  >();\n\n  const inputsArray = (\n    Array.isArray(board.inputsForSerialization)\n      ? input.id : undefined) ??\n        autoId();\n\n      inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo.set(input, {\n        nodeId: inputNodeId,\n        portName: mainInputName,\n      });\n      unconnectedInputs.add(input);\n      const { schema, required } = describeInput(input);\n      let inputNode = inputNodes.get(inputNodeId);\n      if (inputNode === undefined) {\n        inputNode = {\n          id: inputNodeId,\n          type: \"input\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const metadata = inputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (metadata !== undefined) {\n          inputNode.metadata = metadata;\n        }\n        inputNodes.set(inputNodeId, inputNode);\n      }\n      const normalizedSchema = sortKeys(schema, [\n        \"type\",\n        \"behavior\",\n        \"title\",\n        \"description\",\n        \"default\",\n        \"examples\",\n        \"anyOf\",\n        \"properties\",\n        \"items\",\n        \"required\",\n        \"additionalProperties\",\n      ]);\n      if (mainInputName === \"*\") {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.additionalProperties = normalizedSchema;\n      } else {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.properties[mainInputName] =\n          normalizedSchema;\n        if (required) {\n          inputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(mainInputName);\n        }\n      }\n      if (isSpecialInput(input)) {\n        magicInputResolutions.set(input, {\n          nodeId: inputNodeId,\n          portName: mainInputName,\n        });\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const outputsArray = Array.isArray(board.outputsForSerialization)\n    ? (isBoardOutput(port) ? port : undefined);\n\n      if (isSerializableOutputPortReference(port)) {\n        port = port[OutputPortGetter];\n      }\n      // TODO(aomarks) Remove cast.\n      outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n        outputNode = {\n          id: outputNodeId,\n          type: \"output\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const nodeMetadata = outputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (nodeMetadata !== undefined) {\n          outputNode.metadata = nodeMetadata;\n        }\n        if (outputs.$bubble) {\n          addBehavior(outputNode.configuration.schema, \"bubble\");\n        }\n\n        outputNodes.set(outputNodeId, outputNode);\n      }\n      const { schema, required } = describeOutput(output);\n      outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n        `Board input \"${inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo.get(input)!.portName}\" ` +\n          `is not reachable from any of its outputs.`\n      );\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (board.describer) {\n    const describerId = embedBoardAndReturnItsId(board.describer);\n    board.metadata ??= {};\n    board.metadata.describer = `#${describerId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (errors.length > 0) {\n    // TODO(aomarks) Refactor this to a Result<> return, because these errors are\n    // expected as part of the normal course of operation.\n    throw new Error(\n      `Error serializing board:\\n\\n${errors.sort().join(\"\\n\\n\")}`\n version: board.version } : {}),\n    ...(board.metadata ? { metadata: board.metadata } : {}),\n    // Sort the nodes and edges for deterministic BGL output.\n    edges: edges.sort((a, b) => {\n      if (a.from != b.from) {\n        return a.from.localeCompare(b.from);\n      }\n      if (a.to != b.to) {\n        return a.to.localeCompare(b.to);\n      }\n      if (a.out != b.out) {\n SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n An inport port\n          // value can never actually be undefined, right?\n          throw new Error(\n            `Internal error: value was undefined for a ${inputPort.node?.type}:${inputPort.name} port.`\n          );\n        } else if (typeof value === \"symbol\") {\n          // TODO(aomarks) Why is this possible in the type system? Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}

They represent the overall\n  // signature of the board.\n  const outputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n\n  // Analyze inputs and remember some things about them that we'll need when we\n  // traverse the outputs.\n  const inputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n  const inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo = new Map<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort,\n    { nodeId: string; portName: string }\n  >();\n\n  const unconnectedInputs = new Set<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort\n  >();\n\n  const inputsArray = (\n    Array.isArray(board.inputsForSerialization)\n      ? outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n        outputNode = {\n          id: outputNodeId,\n          type: \"output\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const nodeMetadata = outputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (nodeMetadata !== undefined) {\n          outputNode.metadata = nodeMetadata;\n        }\n        if (outputs.$bubble) {\n          addBehavior(outputNode.configuration.schema, \"bubble\");\n        }\n\n        outputNodes.set(outputNodeId, outputNode);\n      }\n      const { schema, required } = describeOutput(output);\n      outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n = embedBoardAndReturnItsId(board.describer);\n    board.metadata ??= {};\n    board.metadata.describer = `#${describerId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (errors.length > 0) {\n    // TODO(aomarks) Refactor this to a if (a.from != b.from) {\n        return a.from.localeCompare(b.from);\n      }\n      if (a.to != b.to) {\n        return a.to.localeCompare(b.to);\n      }\n      if (a.out != b.out) {\n SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}

They represent the overall\n  // signature of the board.\n  const outputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n\n  // Analyze inputs and remember some things about them that we'll need when we\n  // traverse the outputs.\n  const inputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n  const inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo = new Map<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort,\n    { nodeId: string; portName: string }\n  >();\n\n  const unconnectedInputs = new Set<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort\n  >();\n\n  const inputsArray = (\n    Array.isArray(board.inputsForSerialization)\n      ? input.id : undefined) ??\n        autoId();\n\n      inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo.set(input, {\n        nodeId: inputNodeId,\n        portName: mainInputName,\n      });\n      unconnectedInputs.add(input);\n      const { schema, required } = describeInput(input);\n      let inputNode = inputNodes.get(inputNodeId);\n      if (inputNode === undefined) {\n        inputNode = {\n          id: inputNodeId,\n          type: \"input\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const metadata = inputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (metadata !== undefined) {\n          inputNode.metadata = metadata;\n        }\n        inputNodes.set(inputNodeId, inputNode);\n      }\n      const normalizedSchema = sortKeys(schema, [\n        \"type\",\n        \"behavior\",\n        \"title\",\n        \"description\",\n        \"default\",\n        \"examples\",\n        \"anyOf\",\n        \"properties\",\n        \"items\",\n        \"required\",\n        \"additionalProperties\",\n      ]);\n      if (mainInputName === \"*\") {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.additionalProperties = normalizedSchema;\n      } else {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.properties[mainInputName] =\n          normalizedSchema;\n        if (required) {\n          inputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(mainInputName);\n        }\n      }\n      if (isSpecialInput(input)) {\n        magicInputResolutions.set(input, {\n          nodeId: inputNodeId,\n          portName: mainInputName,\n        });\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const outputsArray = Array.isArray(board.outputsForSerialization)\n    ? outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n        outputNode = {\n          id: outputNodeId,\n          type: \"output\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const nodeMetadata = outputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (nodeMetadata !== undefined) {\n          outputNode.metadata = nodeMetadata;\n        }\n        if (outputs.$bubble) {\n          addBehavior(outputNode.configuration.schema, \"bubble\");\n        }\n\n        outputNodes.set(outputNodeId, outputNode);\n      }\n      const { schema, required } = describeOutput(output);\n      outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n = embedBoardAndReturnItsId(board.describer);\n    board.metadata ??= {};\n    board.metadata.describer = `#${describerId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (errors.length > 0) {\n    // TODO(aomarks) Refactor this to a if (a.from != b.from) {\n        return a.from.localeCompare(b.from);\n      }\n      if (a.to != b.to) {\n        return a.to.localeCompare(b.to);\n      }\n      if (a.out != b.out) {\n SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n An inport port\n          // value can never actually be undefined, right?\n          throw new Error(\n            `Internal error: value was undefined for a ${inputPort.node?.type}:${inputPort.name} port.`\n          );\n        } else if (typeof value === \"symbol\") {\n          // TODO(aomarks) Why is this possible in the type system? Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}

They represent the overall\n  // signature of the board.\n  const outputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n\n  // Analyze inputs and remember some things about them that we'll need when we\n  // traverse the outputs.\n  const inputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n  const inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo = new Map<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort,\n    { nodeId: string; portName: string }\n  >();\n\n  const unconnectedInputs = new Set<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort\n  >();\n\n  const inputsArray = (\n    Array.isArray(board.inputsForSerialization)\n      ? input.id : undefined) ??\n        autoId();\n\n      inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo.set(input, {\n        nodeId: inputNodeId,\n        portName: mainInputName,\n      });\n      unconnectedInputs.add(input);\n      const { schema, required } = describeInput(input);\n      let inputNode = inputNodes.get(inputNodeId);\n      if (inputNode === undefined) {\n        inputNode = {\n          id: inputNodeId,\n          type: \"input\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const metadata = inputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (metadata !== undefined) {\n          inputNode.metadata = metadata;\n        }\n        inputNodes.set(inputNodeId, inputNode);\n      }\n      const normalizedSchema = sortKeys(schema, [\n        \"type\",\n        \"behavior\",\n        \"title\",\n        \"description\",\n        \"default\",\n        \"examples\",\n        \"anyOf\",\n        \"properties\",\n        \"items\",\n        \"required\",\n        \"additionalProperties\",\n      ]);\n      if (mainInputName === \"*\") {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.additionalProperties = normalizedSchema;\n      } else {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.properties[mainInputName] =\n          normalizedSchema;\n        if (required) {\n          inputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(mainInputName);\n        }\n      }\n      if (isSpecialInput(input)) {\n        magicInputResolutions.set(input, {\n          nodeId: inputNodeId,\n          portName: mainInputName,\n        });\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const outputsArray = Array.isArray(board.outputsForSerialization)\n    ? outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n        outputNode = {\n          id: outputNodeId,\n          type: \"output\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const nodeMetadata = outputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (nodeMetadata !== undefined) {\n          outputNode.metadata = nodeMetadata;\n        }\n        if (outputs.$bubble) {\n          addBehavior(outputNode.configuration.schema, \"bubble\");\n        }\n\n        outputNodes.set(outputNodeId, outputNode);\n      }\n      const { schema, required } = describeOutput(output);\n      outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n = embedBoardAndReturnItsId(board.describer);\n    board.metadata ??= {};\n    board.metadata.describer = `#${describerId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (errors.length > 0) {\n    // TODO(aomarks) Refactor this to a if (a.from != b.from) {\n        return a.from.localeCompare(b.from);\n      }\n      if (a.to != b.to) {\n        return a.to.localeCompare(b.to);\n      }\n      if (a.out != b.out) {\n SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}

outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n        outputNode = {\n          id: outputNodeId,\n          type: \"output\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const nodeMetadata = outputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (nodeMetadata !== undefined) {\n          outputNode.metadata = nodeMetadata;\n        }\n        if (outputs.$bubble) {\n          addBehavior(outputNode.configuration.schema, \"bubble\");\n        }\n\n        outputNodes.set(outputNodeId, outputNode);\n      }\n      const { schema, required } = describeOutput(output);\n      outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n = embedBoardAndReturnItsId(board.describer);\n    board.metadata ??= {};\n    board.metadata.describer = `#${describerId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (errors.length > 0) {\n    // TODO(aomarks) Refactor this to a SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}

They represent the overall\n  // signature of the board.\n  const outputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n\n  // Analyze inputs and remember some things about them that we'll need when we\n  // traverse the outputs.\n  const inputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n  const inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo = new Map<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort,\n    { nodeId: string; portName: string }\n  >();\n\n  const unconnectedInputs = new Set<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort\n  >();\n\n  const inputsArray = (\n    Array.isArray(board.inputsForSerialization)\n      ? input.id : undefined) ??\n        autoId();\n\n      inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo.set(input, {\n        nodeId: inputNodeId,\n        portName: mainInputName,\n      });\n      unconnectedInputs.add(input);\n      const { schema, required } = describeInput(input);\n      let inputNode = inputNodes.get(inputNodeId);\n      if (inputNode === undefined) {\n        inputNode = {\n          id: inputNodeId,\n          type: \"input\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const metadata = inputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (metadata !== undefined) {\n          inputNode.metadata = metadata;\n        }\n        inputNodes.set(inputNodeId, inputNode);\n      }\n      const normalizedSchema = sortKeys(schema, [\n        \"type\",\n        \"behavior\",\n        \"title\",\n        \"description\",\n        \"default\",\n        \"examples\",\n        \"anyOf\",\n        \"properties\",\n        \"items\",\n        \"required\",\n        \"additionalProperties\",\n      ]);\n      if (mainInputName === \"*\") {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.additionalProperties = normalizedSchema;\n      } else {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.properties[mainInputName] =\n          normalizedSchema;\n        if (required) {\n          inputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(mainInputName);\n        }\n      }\n      if (isSpecialInput(input)) {\n        magicInputResolutions.set(input, {\n          nodeId: inputNodeId,\n          portName: mainInputName,\n        });\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const outputsArray = Array.isArray(board.outputsForSerialization)\n    ? outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n        outputNode = {\n          id: outputNodeId,\n          type: \"output\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const nodeMetadata = outputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (nodeMetadata !== undefined) {\n          outputNode.metadata = nodeMetadata;\n        }\n        if (outputs.$bubble) {\n          addBehavior(outputNode.configuration.schema, \"bubble\");\n        }\n\n        outputNodes.set(outputNodeId, outputNode);\n      }\n      const { schema, required } = describeOutput(output);\n      outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n = embedBoardAndReturnItsId(board.describer);\n    board.metadata ??= {};\n    board.metadata.describer = `#${describerId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (errors.length > 0) {\n    // TODO(aomarks) Refactor this to a Result<> return, because these errors are\n    // expected as part of the normal course of operation.\n    throw new Error(\n      `Error serializing board:\\n\\n${errors.sort().join(\"\\n\\n\")}`\n version: board.version } : {}),\n    ...(board.metadata ? { metadata: board.metadata } : {}),\n    // Sort the nodes and edges for deterministic BGL output.\n    edges: edges.sort((a, b) => {\n      if (a.from != b.from) {\n        return a.from.localeCompare(b.from);\n      }\n      if (a.to != b.to) {\n        return a.to.localeCompare(b.to);\n      }\n      if (a.out != b.out) {\n SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n An inport port\n          // value can never actually be undefined, right?\n          throw new Error(\n            `Internal error: value was undefined for a ${inputPort.node?.type}:${inputPort.name} port.`\n          );\n        } else if (typeof value === \"symbol\") {\n          // TODO(aomarks) Why is this possible in the type system? Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}

They represent the overall\n  // signature of the board.\n  const outputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n\n  // Analyze inputs and remember some things about them that we'll need when we\n  // traverse the outputs.\n  const inputNodes = new Map<string, InputOrOutputNodeDescriptor>();\n  const inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo = new Map<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort,\n    { nodeId: string; portName: string }\n  >();\n\n  const unconnectedInputs = new Set<\n    | Input<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | InputWithDefault<JsonSerializable | undefined>\n    | StarInputs\n    | SerializableInputPort\n  >();\n\n  const inputsArray = (\n    Array.isArray(board.inputsForSerialization)\n      ? input.id : undefined) ??\n        autoId();\n\n      inputObjectsToInputNodeInfo.set(input, {\n        nodeId: inputNodeId,\n        portName: mainInputName,\n      });\n      unconnectedInputs.add(input);\n      const { schema, required } = describeInput(input);\n      let inputNode = inputNodes.get(inputNodeId);\n      if (inputNode === undefined) {\n        inputNode = {\n          id: inputNodeId,\n          type: \"input\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const metadata = inputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (metadata !== undefined) {\n          inputNode.metadata = metadata;\n        }\n        inputNodes.set(inputNodeId, inputNode);\n      }\n      const normalizedSchema = sortKeys(schema, [\n        \"type\",\n        \"behavior\",\n        \"title\",\n        \"description\",\n        \"default\",\n        \"examples\",\n        \"anyOf\",\n        \"properties\",\n        \"items\",\n        \"required\",\n        \"additionalProperties\",\n      ]);\n      if (mainInputName === \"*\") {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.additionalProperties = normalizedSchema;\n      } else {\n        inputNode.configuration.schema.properties[mainInputName] =\n          normalizedSchema;\n        if (required) {\n          inputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(mainInputName);\n        }\n      }\n      if (isSpecialInput(input)) {\n        magicInputResolutions.set(input, {\n          nodeId: inputNodeId,\n          portName: mainInputName,\n        });\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const outputsArray = Array.isArray(board.outputsForSerialization)\n    ? (isBoardOutput(port) ? port : undefined);\n\n      if (isSerializableOutputPortReference(port)) {\n        port = port[OutputPortGetter];\n      }\n      // TODO(aomarks) Remove cast.\n      outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n        outputNode = {\n          id: outputNodeId,\n          type: \"output\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n              required: [],\n              // TODO(aomarks) Disallow extra properties?\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        const nodeMetadata = outputs.$metadata as {\n          title?: string;\n          description?: string;\n        };\n        if (nodeMetadata !== undefined) {\n          outputNode.metadata = nodeMetadata;\n        }\n        if (outputs.$bubble) {\n          addBehavior(outputNode.configuration.schema, \"bubble\");\n        }\n\n        outputNodes.set(outputNodeId, outputNode);\n      }\n      const { schema, required } = describeOutput(output);\n      outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n = embedBoardAndReturnItsId(board.describer);\n    board.metadata ??= {};\n    board.metadata.describer = `#${describerId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (errors.length > 0) {\n    // TODO(aomarks) Refactor this to a Result<> return, because these errors are\n    // expected as part of the normal course of operation.\n    throw new Error(\n      `Error serializing board:\\n\\n${errors.sort().join(\"\\n\\n\")}`\n version: board.version } : {}),\n    ...(board.metadata ? { metadata: board.metadata } : {}),\n    // Sort the nodes and edges for deterministic BGL output.\n    edges: edges.sort((a, b) => {\n      if (a.from != b.from) {\n        return a.from.localeCompare(b.from);\n      }\n      if (a.to != b.to) {\n        return a.to.localeCompare(b.to);\n      }\n      if (a.out != b.out) {\n SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n An inport port\n          // value can never actually be undefined, right?\n          throw new Error(\n            `Internal error: value was undefined for a ${inputPort.node?.type}:${inputPort.name} port.`\n          );\n        } else if (typeof value === \"symbol\") {\n          // TODO(aomarks) Why is this possible in the type system? Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}

outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n        outputNode = {\n          id: outputNodeId,\n          type: \"output\",\n          configuration: {\n            schema: {\n              type: \"object\",\n              properties: {},\n        description?: string;\n        };\n        if (nodeMetadata !== undefined) {\n          outputNode.metadata = nodeMetadata;\n        }\n        if (outputs.$bubble) {\n          addBehavior(outputNode.configuration.schema, \"bubble\");\n        }\n\n        outputNodes.set(outputNodeId, outputNode);\n      }\n      const { schema, required } = describeOutput(output);\n      outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n = embedBoardAndReturnItsId(board.describer);\n    board.metadata ??= {};\n    board.metadata.describer = `#${describerId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (errors.length > 0) {\n    // TODO(aomarks) Refactor this to a SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}

outputNodeId ??= outputs.$id as string | undefined;\n      outputNodeId ??= autoId();\n\n      let outputNode = outputNodes.get(outputNodeId);\n      if (outputNode === undefined) {\n outputNode.configuration.schema.properties[name] = schema;\n      if (deprecated) {\n        addBehavior(schema, \"deprecated\");\n      }\n      if (required) {\n        outputNode.configuration.schema.required.push(name);\n      }\n      if (nested !== undefined) {\n        const { innerBoard, innerPortName } = nested;\n        addEdge(\n          visitNodeAndReturnItsId(innerBoard),\n          innerPortName,\n          outputNodeId,\n          name,\n          isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      } else if resolution.nodeId,\n            resolution.portName,\n            outputNodeId,\n            name,\n            isConstant(output),\n            !required\n          );\n        }\n      } else if isConstant(output),\n          !required\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (unconnectedInputs.size > 0) {\n    for (const input of unconnectedInputs.values()) {\n      errors.push(\n SerializableNode | OldBoardInstance<BoardInputPorts, BoardOutputPorts>\n  ): string {\n    let descriptor = nodes.get(node);\n    if (descriptor !== undefined) {\n      return descriptor.id;\n    }\n Number.MAX_VALUE : indexB)\n        );\n      }\n      return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n    })\n  ) as T;\n}\n\nfunction addBehavior(\n  schema: Schema | JSONSchema4,\n  behavior: BehaviorSchema\n): void {\n  if (schema.behavior === undefined) {\n    schema.behavior = [behavior];\n  } else if (!schema.behavior.includes(behavior)) {\n    schema.behavior.push(behavior);\n    schema.behavior.sort();\n  }\n}\n"]}
